</span></span>\n}}\nThis mixed [[Fish|fish]] [[Soup|soup]] from Tunisia is more like a [[Stew|stew]], so could also be served as a [[Main course|main course]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 2 kg mixed [[Fish and seafood|fish and seafood]], skinned, boned, peeled etc and cut into small pieces, if necessary\n| 4 [[Onions|onions]], roughly chopped\n| 75 ml [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 1 large [[Green pepper|green pepper]], deseeded and chopped\n| 1 large [[Red pepper|red pepper]], deseeded and chopped\n| [[Garlic]], to taste, peeled and findly [[Diced|diced]]\n| 3 [[Litres|litres]] [[Fish stock|fish stock]], water or [[Court bouillon|court bouillon]]\n| 4 large [[Potatoes|potatoes]], cut into smallish chunks\n| 2 bulbs [[Fennel|fennel]], with leaves, [[Diced|diced]]\n| [[Salt]], to taste\n| Large pinch [[Saffron|saffron]], pounded\n| 1 teaspoon [[Ground cumin|ground cumin]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Ground cinnamon|ground cinnamon]]\n| 2 teaspoons [[Harissa|harissa]], or to taste\n| 2 [[Preserved lemons|preserved lemons]], finely chopped\n| 8 [[Tomatoes, peeled|tomatoes, peeled]] and chopped\n| 1 large bunch [[Parsley|parsley]], finely chopped\n| 1 large bunch [[Coriander leaves|coriander leaves]], finely chopped\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]] in a large pan and [[Fry|fry]] the [[Onions|onions]] until soft.\n| Add the [[Peppers|peppers]] and [[Garlic|garlic]] and when the peppers are soft, add the [[Fish stock|fish stock]], water or [[Court bouillon|court bouillon]].\n| Stir in the [[Potatoes|potatoes]], [[Salt|salt]], [[Saffron|saffron]], [[Cumin|cumin]], [[Cinnamon|cinnamon]], [[Harissa|harissa]] and [[Preserved lemons|preserved lemons]] and [[Simmer|simmer]], covered, for about 30 minutes.\n| Add the [[Fish|fish]], [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] and [[Herbs|herbs]] and add further liquid if necessary and cook for a few minutes until the fish is done.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with [[Bread|bread]].\n===Variations===\nYou can also add 2 tablespoons of [[Capers|capers]], 2 tablespoons of [[Caraway seeds|caraway seeds]] and/or 1 teaspoon [[Ground coriander|ground coriander]].  Use the [[Juice|juice]] of 1&frac12; [[Lemons|lemons]] instead of the [[Preserved lemons|preserved lemons]] and if you do not have any [[Harissa|harissa]], substitute it with 1 teaspoon [[Paprika|paprika]] and &frac12; teaspoon [[Cayenne pepper]].\n===Chef's notes===\nUse a mixture of firm [[Fish|fish]], eg [[Monkfish|monkfish]], [[Gurnard|gurnard]], [[Bream|bream]] or [[Bass|bass]] and some delicate fish, eg whiting, [[Cod|cod]] or [[Haddock|haddock]], together with small whole fish, [[Eel|eel]] chunks, [[Squid|squid]], [[Prawns|prawns]] or [[Crabmeat|crabmeat]].\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Broudou bil hout (fish soup)]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Broudou bil hout (fish soup)]]\n[[Category:North African recipes|Broudou bil hout (fish soup)]]\n[[Category:Potato recipes|Broudou bil hout (fish soup)]]\n[[Category:Sea fish recipes|Broudou bil hout (fish soup)]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites|Broudou bil hout (fish soup)]]\n[[Category:Soup and stock recipes|Broudou bil hout (fish soup)]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes|Broudou bil hout (fish soup)]]\n[[Category:Stews and casseroles|Broudou bil hout (fish soup)]]\n[[Category:Starters|Broudou bil hout (fish soup)]]\n[[Category:Tunisian recipes|Broudou bil hout (fish soup)]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered|Bro]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#harissa #fish #preservedlemons #garlic #fishstock #diced #saffron #courtbouillon #potatoes #onions #monkfish </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

[[Cucumber|cucumber]], coarsely chopped\n| 115 g [[Feta]] or [[Caerphilly cheese]], crumbled\n| [[Salt]] and [[Black pepper|black pepper]], to taste\n| [[Lime wedges]], to garnish\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Place the [[Bulgur wheat|bulghur wheat]] in a with the [[Boiling|boiling]] water and leave to soak for 30 minutes. \n| Stir occasionally with a fork, until all the water has been absorbed.\n| Meanwhile, mix together the [[Oil|oil]], [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]] and seasonings in a bowl. \n| Pour this over the [[Bulgur wheat|bulghur wheat]] mixture and stir to combine. \n| Add the [[Herbs|herbs]], mix well, then add the remaining ingredients. \n| Toss to combine then cover and chill until needed. \n| Serve in a bowl, garnished with the [[Lime wedges|lime wedges]].\n}}\n===Variations===\nI would probably add a [[Chilli|chilli]] or two to the [[Salad|salad]].\n\nI used vegetable stock instead of water, added 3 cloves of crushed garlic to the wheat at the soaking stage so the harshness of raw garlic was removed.  \nI found some nice fresh [[sorrel]] leaves whilst [[herb]]-hunting in the garden so added those too along with a spare tomato.  A very nice and colourful salad which will be made again. --[[User:Chef|Chef]] 07:36, 6 March 2011 (GMT)\n===Chef's notes===\nWhen making this as a main meal for two people, I used 200g of bulgur wheat, vegetables as listed and an unmeasured quantity of cheese and there was very little left over.  I would be tempted to increase the amount of bulgur wheat if making this for four people.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Bulghur wheat salad]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments|Bulghur wheat salad]]\n[[Category:Algerian recipes|Bulghur wheat salad]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes|Bulghur wheat salad]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes|Bulghur wheat salad]]\n[[Category:North African recipes|Bulghur wheat salad]]\n[[Category:Salad recipes|Bulghur wheat salad]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites|Bulghur wheat salad]]\n[[Category:Starters|Bulghur wheat salad]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes|Bulghur wheat salad]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes|Bulghur wheat salad]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#bulghurwheatsalad #lemonjuice #limewedges #herbs #cucumber #bulgurwheat #boiling #salad #herb #cheese #unusualrecipes </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Butternut Squash Soup with Rose Harissa",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Butternut Squash Soup with Rose Harissa - Chili soup recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#soup #butternutsquashsoupwithroseharissa #arganoil #boiling #squash #redonion #pumpkins #boiledorsimmered #wintersquash #blender #cream \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Any variety of summer squash or winter squash would work well as a replacement for butternut squash - even pumpkins\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 456\n|PortionCalories = 114\n|DatePublished=22nd January 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 30 minutes\n |PrepTime = 10 minutes\n |CookTime = 20 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Butternut Squash Soup with Rose Harissa recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Difficult ingredients</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Argan oil can be rather hard to find, but you can get it easily on-line.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Image:Squash type.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Harlequin F1 squash would work instead of the butternut squash]]\nAny variety of [[Summer squash|summer squash]] or [[Winter squash|winter squash]] would work well as a replacement for [[Butternut squash|butternut squash]] - even [[Pumpkins|pumpkins]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 2 tablespoons Belazu [[Argan Oil]] \n| 1 [[Red onion|red onion]], sliced \n| 300g [[Squash|squash]], cut into 2.5cm (1in) [[Dice|dice]] \n| 1 [[Vegetable Stock|vegetable stock]] cube \n| 300ml [[Boiling|boiling]] water \n| 2 tablespoons of [[Single cream]] or [[Double cream|double cream]] \n| Rose [[Harissa paste]] (to taste)\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Heat the [[argan oil]] in a saucepan, add the sliced [[Red onion|red onion]] and cook for 2-3 minutes. \n| Add the [[Squash|squash]], [[Fry|fry]] for a further 2-3 minutes. \n| Dissolve the [[Stock cube|stock cube]] in the [[Boiling|boiling]] water, and add to the pan. \n| Raise the heat, and when the [[Soup|soup]] begins to [[Boil|boil]], lower the heat to a rapid simmer. [[Simmer]] for 10-12 minutes. \n| Place the hot [[Soup|soup]] carefully into a [[Blender|blender]], and blend until smooth. \n| Stir a swirl (approx &frac14; level teaspoons but depends on how spicy you like your [[Soup|soup]]!) of Rose [[Harissa]] onto each serving along with a swirl of [[Cream|cream]] and serve.\n}}\n\n{{Template:Belazu attribution}}\n===Belazu products used in this recipe===\n* [http://www.mybelazu.com/details/argan-oil.html Belazu Argan Oil]\n* [http://www.mybelazu.com/details/rose-harissa.html Belazu Rose Harissa]\n\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Belazu recipes]]\n[[Category:Recipes from other sites]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Middle Eastern recipes]]\n[[Category:Moroccan recipes]]\n[[Category:North African recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Soup and stock recipes]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Squash recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#soup #butternutsquashsoupwithroseharissa #arganoil #boiling #squash #redonion #pumpkins #boiledorsimmered #wintersquash #blender #cream </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

Variations of this dish are also popular in Algeria and Tunisia.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| [[Olive oil]] for [[Frying|frying]]\n| [[Garlic]] cloves, to taste, chopped\n| 1 [[Onion|onion]], chopped\n| [[Green chillies]], to taste, finely chopped\n| 5 ripe [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], sliced\n| Seasoning\n| 4 large [[Eggs|eggs]]\n}}\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Heat the [[Olive oil|olive oil]] in a [[Frying pan|frying pan]] and gently [[Fry|fry]] the [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Onion|onion]] until soft and golden [[Brown|brown]] (about 10 minutes). \n| Mix in the [[Chillies|chillies]] then arrange the [[Tomato|tomato]] slices on top. \n| Season, then cover and [[Simmer|simmer]] gently for about 15 minutes.\n| Break the [[Eggs|eggs]] into the pan and, using a fork, spread the whites to cover the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]]. \n| Cover and cook for about 6 minutes, or until the [[Eggs|eggs]] are done.\n| Cut the mixture into quarters and scoop these out onto warmed serving plates.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with [[Pitta bread|pitta bread]].\n===Variations===\nAdd a little [[Tomato|tomato]] pur\u00e9e to the mixture with the [[Chillies|chillies]] for additional colour or try adding a teaspoon of [[Hilba|hilba]] to it. You can also include [[sweet peppers]].  In North Africa [[merguez]] is sometimes added.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Chakchouka (eggs, tomatoes and chillies)]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes|Chakchouka (eggs, tomatoes and chillies)]]\n[[Category:Egg recipes|Chakchouka (eggs, tomatoes and chillies)]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes|Chakchouka (eggs, tomatoes and chillies)]]\n[[Category:Libyan recipes|Chakchouka (eggs, tomatoes and chillies)]]\n[[Category:Middle Eastern recipes]]\n[[Category:North African recipes|Chakchouka (eggs, tomatoes and chillies)]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites|Chakchouka (eggs, tomatoes and chillies)]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes|Chakchouka (eggs, tomatoes and chillies)]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes|Chakchouka (eggs, tomatoes and chillies)]]\n[[Category:Breakfast recipes]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#eggs #chillies #onion #oliveoil #tomatoes #tomato #garlic #pittabread #sweetpeppers #fry #hilba </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Chalda loubia khadra (Green beans with almonds)",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Chalda loubia khadra (Green beans with almonds) an egg recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#mayonnaise #beans #salad #parsley #gravadlax #almonds #greenbeans #pile #toasted #groundcumin #unusualrecipes \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=An unusual salad from Algeria\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1880\n|PortionCalories = 470\n|DatePublished=21st January 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = Chalda loubia khadra, served with [[gravadlax]]\n |Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 20 minutes\n |PrepTime = 10 minutes  \n |CookTime = 10 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Chalda loubia khadra (Green beans with almonds) recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Algerian salad</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Almost a main meal</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Klapaucius|Klapaucius]] </span></span>\n}}\nAn unusual [[Salad|salad]] from Algeria.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 675 g fine [[Green beans|green beans]], top and tailed\n| 3 tablespoons [[Parsley|parsley]], finely chopped\n| 150 ml [[Mayonnaise|mayonnaise]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Ground cumin|ground cumin]]\n| 4 [[Hard boiled eggs|hard boiled eggs]], thinly sliced\n| 50 g slivered [[Almonds|almonds]], [[Toasted|toasted]] until golden\n| [[Black olives]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Cook the [[Beans|beans]] in lightly [[Salted|salted]] water for 8-10 minutes.\n| Strain and leave to cool.\n| Mix the [[Parsley|parsley]], [[Mayonnaise|mayonnaise]] and [[Cumin|cumin]] in a bowl.\n| Add the [[Beans|beans]] and toss gently.\n| Taste, and adjust seasoning if necessary.\n| [[Pile]] the mixture into the centre of a shallow dish.\n| Arrange the [[Egg|egg]] slices around the edge and scatter the [[Almonds|almonds]] and [[Olives|olives]] over the top.\n| Serve immediately.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nAlthough designed to be an [[Accompaniment|accompaniment]], I see no reason why this recipe should not be served as a [[Main course|main course]] [[Salad|salad]] for 2. With some [[Bread|bread]] it would be a very balanced and healthy meal.\n===Variations===\nInstead of normal [[Mayonnaise|mayonnaise]], I like to use [[Not-for-wimps garlic mayonnaise]] for a bit more bite.\n===Chef's notes===\nDo not overcook the [[Beans|beans]] - they are much better if they are '[[Al dente|al dente]]'.\n\nI made this recipe using homegrown baby [[runner beans]].  As there were not that many of them, I made up the difference with frozen peas and served it with [[gravadlax]] and homegrown [[cucumbers]]. --[[User:Chef|Chef]] 09:44, 13 July 2011 (BST)\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Chalda loubia khadra (green beans with almonds)]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments|Chalda loubia khadra (green beans with almonds)]]\n[[Category:Algerian recipes|Chalda loubia khadra (green beans with almonds)]]\n[[Category:Egg recipes|Chalda loubia khadra (green beans with almonds)]]\n[[Category:North African recipes|Chalda loubia khadra (green beans with almonds)]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites|Chalda loubia khadra (green beans with almonds)]]\n[[Category:Starters|Chalda loubia khadra (green beans with almonds)]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes|Chalda loubia khadra (green beans with almonds)]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes|Chalda loubia khadra (green beans with almonds)]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#mayonnaise #beans #salad #parsley #gravadlax #almonds #greenbeans #pile #toasted #groundcumin #unusualrecipes </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Chermoula",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Chermoula, Sauce recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#chermoula #garlic #marinade #coriander #groundcumin #fish #herbs #saffronstrands #tagine #paprika #lemonjuice \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Chermoula or charmoula is a marinade used in Algerian, Moroccan and Tunisian cooking\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 42\n|PortionCalories = 10\n|DatePublished=20th December 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 4 - Will marinade meat for 4 to 6 people\n |Difficulty = 1\n |ImageComment = [[Tagine]] cooked with chermoula [[marinade]]\n |TotalTime = 10 minutes\n |PrepTime = 10 minutes\n |CookTime = None\n|Image = [[Image:Chermoula.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Best on Basa</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Nice fish marinade with easy to find ingredients</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Klapaucius|Klapaucius]] </span></span>\n}}\nChermoula or charmoula is a [[marinade]] used in [[Algerian]], [[Moroccan]] and [[Tunisian]] cooking. It is usually used to flavour [[fish]] or [[seafood]], but it can be used on other [[meats]] or [[vegetables]].\n\nChermoula is often made of a mixture of [[herbs]], [[oil]], [[lemon juice]], [[preserved lemons]], [[Garlic|garlic]], [[cumin]], and [[salt]]. It may also include [[onion]], fresh [[coriander]], ground [[chilli peppers]], [[black pepper]], or [[saffron]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 2 tablespoons roughly chopped [[Coriander|coriander]] \n| 3 [[Garlic|garlic]] cloves, chopped \n| 1 &frac12; teaspoons [[Ground cumin|ground cumin]] \n| &frac12; medium-hot long red [[Chilli|chilli]], seeded and chopped \n| &frac12; teaspoon [[Saffron strands|saffron strands]] \n| 80ml [[Extra virgin olive oil|extra virgin olive oil]] \n| [[Juice]] of 1 [[Lemon|lemon]] \n| &frac12; teaspoon [[Paprika|paprika]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| To make [[chermoula]], place all ingredients into a [[Food processor|food processor]] and process until smooth. Season with [[Salt|salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]].\n}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Algerian recipes]]\n[[Category:Moroccan recipes]]\n[[Category:North African recipes]]\n[[Category:Tunisian recipes]]\n[[Category:Dips and sauces]]\n[[Category:Ingredients]]\n[[Category:Prepared foods]]\n[[Category:Store cupboard items]]\n[[Category:Uncooked]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#chermoula #garlic #marinade #coriander #groundcumin #fish #herbs #saffronstrands #tagine #paprika #lemonjuice </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

''See: [[Boiled chicken pieces]].''\n| Big handful of fresh [[Parsley|parsley]], chopped\n| 25 g shelled [[Pistachio nuts|pistachio nuts]], (about 50 g with shells) \n| Greek [[Yogurt|yogurt]] for garnish\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]] and gently saut\u00e9 the [[Onions|onions]] and [[Garlic|garlic]] for 4 minutes\n| Add the [[Chili|chili]] and a grind of [[Pepper|pepper]] and [[Fry|fry]] for a minute just to flavour the [[Oil|oil]]\n| Add the [[Rice|rice]] and stir well to coat with [[Oil|oil]]\n| Mix the [[Orange juice|orange juice]], [[Apricots|apricots]] and the [[Stock|stock]], add to the [[Rice|rice]] and bring to the [[Boil|boil]]\n| Reduce the heat, cover and [[Simmer|simmer]] on a low heat for 20 minutes.  Don't stir the [[Rice|rice]] during this time\n| Stir the [[Chicken|chicken]] pieces, [[Parsley|parsley]], [[Orange|orange]] [[Zest|zest]] and the [[Pistachio nuts|pistachio nuts]]. Cook for a few minutes until the chicken is reheated\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with [[Greek yogurt]] as a [[Side dish|side dish]]\n==See also==\n* {{See also - Jointing a chicken}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Middle Eastern recipes]]\n[[Category:North African recipes]]\n[[Category:Rice recipes]]\n[[Category:Fruit recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#chicken #rice #parsley #garlic #zest #orangejuice #orange #chickenandorangepilaf #pistachionuts #boiledchickenpieces #onion </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

358\n|DatePublished=23rd June 2014\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 6\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime = 1 day, 8 hours\n|PrepTime = 1 day\n|CookTime = 8 hours\n|Image = [[Image:Chicken k'dra with Chickpeas, red peppers and raisins recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Can't be for Christmas then?</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:NonLoggedInUser|NonLoggedInUser]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Image:Turkey instead of chicken.jpg|thumb|300px|right|A whole turkey leg [1400g] instead of a small chicken]]\nTypical of a lot of [[North African]] recipes, this is a fruity and spicy dish with lots of [[Onions|onions]], but not necessarily hot.\n\nIf you don't have a [[Slow cooker|slow cooker]], [[Chicken kadra with Chickpeas, red peppers and raisins|we have a cooker top version of the same recipe]].\n\nUnless you are using canned [[Chick-peas|chick-peas]], you will need to soak the [[Chick peas|chick peas]] overnight.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 1 [[Chicken|chicken]] cut into about 6 pieces, [[Jointing a chicken|it's very easy to do, see here]]\n| 175g of [[Dried|dried]] [[Chick peas|chick peas]], soaked overnight in cold water, well rinsed and drained\n| 6 medium [[Onions|onions]], peeled and chopped.  About 450g when chopped.  A [[food processor]] is ideal for this task!\n| 2 pinches of [[Saffron|saffron]]\n| 2 [[Cinnamon sticks|cinnamon sticks]]\n| 1 fresh [[bay leaf]]\n| A pinch of [[mixed herbs]]\n| A pinch of [[chilli flakes]]\n| Half a teaspoon of [[chilli flakes]]\n| 850 ml (1.5 pints) of [[Chicken stock]]\n| 2 tablespoons [[Smen|smen]] or [[Ghee|ghee]]\n| 2 [[sweet peppers|red peppers]], [[Roasted sweet peppers| roasted, deseeded and slices, see here]]\n| Half a 1 teaspoon [[Sea Salt|sea salt]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Black pepper|black pepper]]\n| 4 tablespoons of chopped [[Dried fruit|dried fruit]] ; [[Raisins|raisins]], [[Sultanas|sultanas]], [[Apricots|apricots]], [[Prunes|prunes]]\n}}\n''' to serve'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| lots of freshly chopped [[Parsley|parsley]]\n| [[Toasted]] [[Almond flakes|almond flakes]]\n| [[Lemon]] wedges\n| Crusty [[Bread|bread]], [[boiled potatoes]] or buttery [[Cous-cous|cous-cous]]\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* [[Roasted sweet peppers|Roast, skin and deseed]] the [[Red peppers|red peppers]] and slice thinly\n* Separate the [[Chicken|chicken]] into 6 pieces, discard the skin\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| To the [[Slow cooker|slow cooker]], add the [[Chicken|chicken]] pieces, the soaked and drained [[Chick peas|chick peas]], half of the chopped [[Onions|onions]], the [[Saffron strands|saffron strands]], [[Cinnamon sticks|cinnamon sticks]], [[Salt|salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]], [[mixed herbs]], [[turmeric]] and [[chilli flakes]].\n| Add the [[Chicken stock|chicken stock]]\n| Stir well and cook, covered for a 8 hours on low.\n| When there is a few hours left, add the remaining [[Onions|onions]], [[Dried fruit|dried fruit]], [[Smen|smen]] or [[Ghee|ghee]] together with half of the chopped [[Parsley|parsley]] and half of the [[Red pepper|sweet pepper]] slices.\n| Cook for a further 2 hours.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe, scattered with the [[Toasted|toasted]] [[Almonds|almonds]] and the remaining [[Parsley|parsley]] and [[Red pepper|red pepper]] slices.  Accompany with the [[Lemon wedges|lemon wedges]].\n\nThis goes well [[boiled potatoes]], crusty [[Bread|bread]] or buttery [[Cous-cous|cous-cous]]\n===Chef's notes===\nThe cost of a whole chicken from Morrisons was nine pounds which seems ridiculous for a supermarket chicken [June 2014].  Next to the chickens was a huge whole turkey leg (in two pieces), weighing in at 1.4 kg.  For less than half the price of a [[chicken]].  \n\nUsing the whole [[turkey]] leg, I amended the recipe slightly to my personal tastes. I also added a [[bay leaf]], half a teaspoon of [[turmeric]], a pinch of [[mixed herbs]] and some [[chilli flakes]] at the start, and reduced the [[ground pepper]] to just a good pinch.  I've skinned the legs and cut 6 deep slashes right down to the bone so they cook evenly.  I added 700ml (1.5 pints) of chicken stock, which did not cover the turkey legs, but they will still cook perfectly well, especially if you turn them at the final hour.  ''I've [[Roasting a chicken in a slow cooker|roasted a whole chicken in a slow cooker]] and it was perfectly cooked (8 hours on low).''   \n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Middle Eastern recipes]]\n[[Category:Moroccan recipes]]\n[[Category:North African recipes]]\n[[Category:Tunisian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Fruit recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes]]\n[[Category:Stewed, braised or pot roasted]]\n[[Category:Slow cooked]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Slow cooker recipes]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#chicken #onions #chilliflakes #mixedherbs #chickpeas #parsley #smen #chickenstock #slowcooker #turmeric #boiledpotatoes </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Chicken tagine with chermoula, Meat recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#chermoula #chicken #preservedlemon #coriander #tagine #onion #belazu #fry #tomatoes #marinade #celery \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Chermoula is often used as a marinade but in this chicken tagine recipe from Australia it is used as a cooking sauce\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 3153\n|PortionCalories = 788\n|DatePublished=19th January 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 2\n |ImageComment = [[Tagine]] cooked with chermoula [[marinade]]\n |TotalTime = 1 hour\n |CookTime = 35 minutes\n |PrepTime = 25 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Chermoula.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n }}\n\n[[Chermoula]] is often used as a [[marinade]] but in this chicken [[tagine]] recipe from Australia it is used as a cooking sauce.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 2 tablespoons [[Extra virgin olive oil|extra virgin olive oil]] \n| 4 (175g each) skinless boned [[Chicken|chicken]] breasts \n| 2 [[Celery|celery]] stalks \n| 1 [[Carrot|carrot]] \n| 1 small [[Onion|onion]] \n| 1 [[Belazu]] [[Preserved lemon|preserved lemon]], finely chopped \n| 4 roma [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], sliced \n| 600ml fresh [[Chicken stock|chicken stock]] \n| 8 small [[New Potatoes|new potatoes]], cut lengthways into quarters \n| 16 [[Belazu]] [[Black olives|black olives]], pitted \n| 1 teaspoon chopped [[Coriander|coriander]] \n| 1 teaspoon chopped [[Mint|mint]] \n}}\n'''Chermoula'''\n* 2 tablespoons roughly chopped [[Coriander|coriander]] \n* 3 [[Garlic|garlic]] cloves, chopped \n* 1 &frac12; teaspoons [[Ground cumin|ground cumin]] \n* &frac12; medium-hot long red [[Chilli|chilli]], seeded and chopped \n* &frac12; teaspoon [[Saffron strands|saffron strands]] \n* 80ml [[Extra virgin olive oil|extra virgin olive oil]] \n* [[Juice]] of 1 [[Lemon|lemon]] \n* &frac12; teaspoon [[Paprika|paprika]]\n\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| To make [[chermoula]], place all ingredients into a [[Food processor|food processor]] and process until smooth. Season with [[Salt|salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]].\n| Heat [[Oil|oil]] in a [[Deep frying|deep frying]] pan. Season [[Chicken|chicken]] breasts on both side with [[Salt|salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]]. Add to pan and [[Fry|fry]] over a medium-high heat for 1-2 minutes or until golden, the turn over and lightly [[Brown|brown]] other side. Transfer to a plate and set aside. \n| Add [[Celery|celery]], [[Carrot|carrot]] and [[Onion|onion]] to the pan and [[Fry|fry]] over a low heat for 5 minutes or until soft but not [[Browned|browned]]. Add half the [[Preserved lemon|preserved lemon]], 2 tablespoons of the [[chermoula]], the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] and [[Stock|stock]]. Return the [[Chicken|chicken]] to the pan, then bring to the [[Boil|boil]]. Reduce heat to low and [[Simmer|simmer]] for 10 minutes.\n| Add [[Potatoes|potatoes]] to pan and cook for a further 6-8 minutes or until potatoes and [[Chicken|chicken]] are cooked through. Stir in [[Olives|olives]], [[Herbs|herbs]] and the remaining [[chermoula]] and [[Preserved lemon|preserved lemon]] into the [[Sauce|sauce]]. Adjust the seasoning if necessary. Lift chicken into warmed deep plates and spoon over sauce. Garnish with extra torn [[Coriander|coriander]] and [[Mint leaves|mint leaves]] and serve with [[Steamed|steamed]] [[Barley|barley]] [[Couscous|couscous]].\n}}\n\n(''Delicious magazine, Australia'')\n\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Can't find my tagine</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.1</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Need to find my tagine as we lost ours after the move. I would love to try this.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n\n\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Tagine]]\n[[Category:Algerian recipes|Tagine]]\n[[Category:Belazu recipes|Tagine]]\n[[Category:Recipes from other sites|Tagine]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Tagine]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes|Tagine]]\n[[Category:Moroccan recipes|Tagine]]\n[[Category:North African recipes|Tagine]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes|Tagine]]\n[[Category:Stews and casseroles|Tagine]]\n[[Category:Tunisian recipes|Tagine]]\n[[Category:Stewed, braised or pot roasted]] \n{{Template:Belazu attribution}}\n\n\n===Belazu products used in this recipe===\n* [http://www.mybelazu.com/details/black-with-herbs.html Belazu Black olives with herbs]\n* [http://www.mybelazu.com/details/belazu-pickled-lemons.html Belazu Preserved Lemon]\n==See also==\n{{Tagine-recipe-list}}\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#chermoula #chicken #preservedlemon #coriander #tagine #onion #belazu #fry #tomatoes #marinade #celery </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

These take a while to prepare but are most definitely worth the effort.  Whatever else you put on the kebab sticks is up to your personal taste.\n\nWe've chosen [[Sweet peppers|sweet peppers]] and [[Mushrooms|mushrooms]].\n\nAs I've recently bought a selection of Mae Ploy [[Curry|curry]] pastes, I've used the Mae Ploy [[Massaman curry]] paste in this recipe.\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n}}\n====kebabs====\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| One massive [[Chicken breast|chicken breast]] fillet\n| Two [[Sweet peppers|sweet peppers]], any colour\n| 24 [[Button mushrooms|button mushrooms]]\n}}\n====marinade====\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 4 [[Cloves of Garlic, peeled and crushed|cloves of garlic, peeled and crushed]]\n| 250g [[Greek yogurt]]\n| 2 teaspoons Mae Play [[Massaman curry]] paste\n| 1 teaspoon soft [[Brown sugar|brown sugar]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Lime juice|lime juice]]\n}}\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n}}\n====marinade====\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Mix all of the [[Marinade|marinade]] ingredients together in a [[Lock & Lock box]] and stir really well to ensure they are properly mixed\n| Cut the [[Chicken|chicken]] into bite-sized pieces and add to the [[Marinade|marinade]]\n| Cover and shake hard so the [[Chicken|chicken]] is evenly coated\n| Leave to [[Marinade|marinade]] for about 5 hours, shaking now and then if you can\n}}\n====kebabs====\n{{RecipeMethod\n| While you assemble the [[Kebabs|kebabs]], preheat you [[Grill|grill]] to maximum\n| Deseed the [[Peppers|peppers]] and cut into squares so they 'fit' the [[Kebabs|kebabs]]\n| Slide the [[Chicken|chicken]], [[Mushrooms|mushrooms]] and [[Pepper|pepper]] slices onto your [[Kebab|kebab]] sticks - metal [[Skewers|skewers]] work well for us\n| Arrange over a [[Foil|foil]]-lined [[Oven tray|oven tray]] and coat with any spare [[Marinade|marinade]]\n| [[Grill]] for 15 minutes, turning once\n| [[Rest for]] 5 minutes before serving\n}}\n\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with [[Vegetable|vegetable]] [[Rice|rice]] or [[Pittas|pittas]] and a [[Salad|salad]]\n===Variations===\n[[Cherry tomatoes]], slices of [[Fruit|fruit]] and slices of [[Red onion|red onion]] and [[Olives|olives]] go well on these [[Kebabs|kebabs]].\n===Chef's notes===\nThese would be perfect for a [[Barbecue|barbecue]] too, though not for us as it's snowing at the moment!\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Greek recipes]]\n[[Category:Indian recipes]]\n[[Category:Middle Eastern recipes]]\n[[Category:North African recipes]]\n[[Category:Thai recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Marinades dressings and butters]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes]]\n[[Category:Barbecue recipes]]\n[[Category:Grilled, griddled or barbecued]]\n[[Category:Marinaded]]\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:12032020'>#marinade #chicken #kebabs #massamancurry #sweetpeppers #chickentikkakebabs #grill #mushrooms #rice #limejuice #olives</code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

the chicken pieces to a clean oven tray and return to the oven for 10 minutes just to crisp the skin\n| [[Bubble]] up the pan juices over a medium to high heat for 3 minutes or so, until reduced a little, mash and sieve to make a delicious [[gravy]].  Add a little [[plain flour]] to thicken if needed. \n| Serve sprinkled with [[parsley]]\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Chicken with Preserved Lemon and Olives browned.jpg|thumb|300px|right|After browning\nImage:Chicken with Preserved Lemon and Olives first cook.jpg|thumb|300px|right|After cooking on the vegetables\n</gallery>\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe the [[Chicken|chicken]] on a bed of [[Barley]] [[Couscous|couscous]], with the [[Sauce|sauce]] spooned over.\n\n{{Template:Belazu attribution}}\n===Belazu products used in this recipe===\n* [http://www.mybelazu.com/details/early-harvest.html Belazu Early Harvest Extra Virgin Olive Oil Unfiltered]\n* [http://www.mybelazu.com/products/extra virgin-olive-oils.html Belazu Extra virgin olive oil]\n* [http://www.mybelazu.com/details/belazu-pickled-lemons.html Belazu Preserved Lemon]\n* [http://www.mybelazu.com/details/traditional-barley-couscous.html Belazu Traditional Barley Couscous]\n\n==See also==\n* {{See also - Jointing a chicken}}\n\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Belazu recipes]]\n[[Category:Recipes from other sites]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Middle Eastern recipes]]\n[[Category:North African recipes]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes]]\n[[Category:Stews and casseroles]]\n[[Category:Stewed, braised or pot roasted]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#chickenwithpreservedlemonandolives #chicken #preservedlemon #couscous #wine #garlic #oliveoil #belazu #barley #casserole #redonions </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Chickpea salad with red onions goats cheese and paprika recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#chickpeas #chickpeasaladwithredonionsgoatscheeseandpaprika #oliveoil #lime #garlic #onions #vacuumpacked #zest #wok #boil #limezest \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Standard Moroccan fare, this vegetarian main course is delicious served with homemade pitta bread. It's sort of like a chunky hummus\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2537\n|PortionCalories = 634\n|DatePublished=13th November 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 4\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime = 1 day, 45 minutes\n|PrepTime = 1 day\n|CookTime =  45 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Chickpea salad with red onions goats cheese and paprika recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Vegetarian loviliness</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.67</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Visually exciting and very tasty.</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Image:Chickpea salad with red onions goats cheese vacuum packed.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Left-overs [[vacuum packed]] and ready to freeze]]\nStandard Moroccan fare, this [[Vegetarian|vegetarian]] [[Main course|main course]] is delicious served with [[Home-made pitta bread|homemade pitta bread]].  It's sort of like a chunky [[hummus]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 225 g of [[Dried|dried]] [[Chick peas|chick peas]] soaked overnight in cold water - 2 drained 400g cans of tinned [[Chickpeas|chickpeas]] is an equivalent amount\n| 1 large [[Red onion|red onion]], peeled and sliced into thin strips\n| 1 teaspoon freshly [[Ground cumin seeds|ground cumin seeds]]\n| Half a teaspoon of dried [[oregano]]\n| 4 large [[Cloves of Garlic, peeled and crushed|cloves of garlic, peeled and crushed]]\n| 2 teaspoons of [[Smoked paprika powder|smoked paprika powder]]\n| 3 tablespoons of [[Olive oil|olive oil]] plus a little extra\n| [[Juice]] and [[Zest|zest]] from 1 fresh [[Lime|lime]]\n| Bunch of fresh [[Parsley leaves|parsley leaves]], washed and finely chopped\n| Bunch of fresh [[Coriander leaves|coriander leaves]], washed and finely chopped\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n}}\n''' to serve'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 125g [[Goats' cheese|goats' cheese]], crumbled\n| 6 [[Home-made pitta breads]]\n\n}}\n\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| If using dried [[Chickpeas|chickpeas]], drain and rinse well, place in a heave saucepan covered with cold water, bring to the [[Boil|boil]] and [[Simmer|simmer]] for 45 minutes.  Drain the [[Boiled|boiled]] [[Peas|peas]] and remove and discard any loose skins.\n| If using canned [[Chickpeas|chickpeas]], just rinse and drain well, they are already cooked.\n| Add the [[Olive oil|olive oil]], [[black pepper]], [[Garlic|garlic]], sliced [[Onions|onions]] to a [[Wok|wok]] or large [[Frying pan|frying pan]] and saut\u00e9 for 5 minutes, just enough to take the edge off the [[Garlic|garlic]] and to caramelise the [[Onions|onions]] a little.\n| Tip in the [[Chickpeas|chickpeas]], [[Paprika|paprika]], [[Ground cumin|ground cumin]], [[Salt|salt]], [[Lime juice|lime juice]] and [[Zest|zest]] together with the [[Herbs|herbs]] and toss well so everything is coated.\n|If you make this ahead of time I would make it without the fresh herbs, [[lime zest]] and [[lime|juice]] but add any extra [[olive oil]], leaving it in the pan or wok for the flavours to amalgamate.  Reheat the pan and add the lime and herbs just before serving.\n|Drizzle with a little extra olive oil if you feel it needs more dressing.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nTransfer to a large serving bowl while warm and top with crumbled [[Goats' cheese|goats' cheese]].\n\nServe with [[Home-made pitta breads|homemade pitta breads]] - they are simple to make and far superior to any shop-bought product.\n===Variations===\nTake 50% of the finished product, with or without 50% of the [[goats' cheese]], and blend in a [[food processor]], then mix back into the whole chick peas for a more interesting texture.\n===Chef's notes===\nAny of the chickpea salad unused on the day would [[freeze]] well, with or without the [[goats' cheese]] provided it is refrigerated the moment it cools.  It would keep in even better condition if it were [[vacuum packed]] first.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Algerian recipes]]\n[[Category:Lebanese recipes]]\n[[Category:Libyan recipes]]\n[[Category:Middle Eastern recipes]]\n[[Category:Moroccan recipes]]\n[[Category:North African recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#chickpeas #chickpeasaladwithredonionsgoatscheeseandpaprika #oliveoil #lime #garlic #onions #vacuumpacked #zest #wok #boil #limezest </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Chorizo orange and apricot couscous",

Don't follow this recipe exactly, be bold and experiment with the ingredients, you won't be disappointed.\n\n'''Frying the chorizo'''\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 150 g (5 oz) dried [[Couscous|couscous]]\n| 250 ml [[Chicken stock|chicken stock]] ( I used some leftover [[Butternut squash bisque]] with a little water, heated in the microwave)\n| 1 [[Onion|onion]], peeled and chopped\n| 2 Cloves of [[Garlic|garlic]], peeled and chopped roughly\n| A very good slug of [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| &#189; small of pack sliced [[Chorizo sausages|chorizo sausages]] and &#189; small pack of sliced peppered [[salami]] (or any interesting spicy 'cold-meat' combination)\n}}\n'''Apricot sauce'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 8 [[Dried apricots|dried apricots]], chopped\n| [[Zest|zest]] of an [[Orange|orange]]\n| Juice, zest and chopped flesh 1 [[Orange|orange]]\n| 4 tablespoons [[Sherry|sherry]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Cumin seeds|cumin seeds]], bruised and crushed, not powdered\n| 1 teaspoon [[Caraway seeds|caraway seeds]], bruised and crushed, not powdered\n| Pinch of [[Salt|salt]]\n| [[Ground black pepper]]\n}}\n'''Salad ingredients'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 1 small [[sweet pepper]], deseeded and chopped (we had loads of miniature coloured sweet peppers that we used this time)\n| 2 fresh [[tomatoes]], chopped\n}}\n'''Garnish'''\n| Handful of shelled [[Pistachio nuts|pistachio nuts]], crushed\n| Bunch of fresh [[Parsley leaves|parsley leaves]], finely chopped\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Bring your [[Stock|stock]] to [[Boiling|boiling]] and pour over the [[Couscous|couscous]], leave to stand for about 15 minutes or until the stock is absorbed\n| [[Fry]] the [[Onions|onions]] and [[Garlic|garlic]] in a good slug of [[Olive oil|olive oil]] for about 5 minutes - the more flavoured [[Oil|oil]] you can get on the [[Couscous|couscous]], the better\n| Roll the [[Meat|meat]] slices and chop into slivers\n| [[Fry]] the [[Meat|meat]] until the [[Fat|fat]] from the [[Meat|meat]] colours your [[Oil|oil]], remove from the heat\n| In a small pan, add the chopped [[Apricots|apricots]], [[Orange|orange]] flesh and juice, crushed [[Spices|spices]], pinch of [[Salt|salt]] and a grind of [[Pepper|pepper]] and gently [[Simmer|simmer]] until the [[Sherry|sherry]] has reduced and all you are left with is a nice sticky goo.\n| Mix the couscous, salad ingredients and apricot sauce together, sprinkle with [[Pistachio nuts|pistachio nuts]] and [[Parsley|parsley]]\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Mergez and pepperoni frying.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Frying and flavouring the oil\nImage:Mergez orange and apricot couscous ingredients.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Fresh ingredients\n</gallery>\n===Serving suggestions===\n\nServe hot, warm or cold\n\n===Chef's note===\n\nAs this dish is all about the taste and texture explosions of all the different ingredients, I find it's better to chop the garlic so you have little taste bites, rather than crush it and just add the general flavour.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:North African recipes]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Fruit recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#couscous #orange #garlic #chorizoorangeandapricotcouscous #fry #pistachionuts #oliveoil #sherry #fat #onions #simmer </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

Finish with some [[Almonds|almonds]].\n| Take the [[Chicken|chicken]] out of the [[Oven|oven]] and serve with the [[Salad|salad]], warm [[Flatbread|flatbread]] and a generous dollop of [[Houmous|houmous]].\n}}\n(''TV Times'')\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Chicken marinaded.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Close and shake well\nImage:Chicken and marinade.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Add the chicken and the [[harissa paste]] mixture to the Lock and lock box.\n</gallery>\n\n===Chef's notes===\nI have not yet tried the [[Belazu]] rose [[Harissa paste|harissa paste]] yet, but it cannot be a strong as my [[Harissa|harissa]] paste recipe. [[Image:RecipeCouscous.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Anne's favourite</span>''\n\n<span couscous\n| 1 Knorr [[chicken stock]] cube \n| 1 bunch fresh [[parsley]], chopped\n| 1 bunch fresh coriander, chopped\n| 6  fresh [[mint]] leaves, chopped\n| 3 \" [[cucumber]] peeled, quartered seeds]], toasted\n| 6 dried apricots, chopped well\n| 2 tablespoons sultanas or raisins\n| 4 tablespoons [[olive oil]]\n| Freshly ground [[black pepper]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Boil [[Harissa lamb|harissa lamb]]. Be authentic, serve with a small bowl of [[Harissa paste|harissa paste]].\n\n===Variations===\n\nSwitch the [[lemon]] for an orange. \n\nAs with most rice or grains, couscous does not have a great deal of flavour so the punch comes from the ingredients it's cooked with.\n\nTry [[sweetcorn]], black olives, [[pine nuts]], [[cashews]], [[red kidney beans]], chopped apples, dates, toasted [[Cashew nuts|cashew nuts]], figs... you get the idea.\n\n===Chef's tip===\n\nUse double the volume of water to volume of couscous\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:North African recipes]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#sesameseeds #harissapaste #lemon #colourfulcouscousrecipe #sweetcorn #blackpepper #cashews #harissalamb #chickenstock #redkidneybeans #parsley </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Couscous, pepper and garlic salad a Spanish recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#couscouspepperandgarlicsalad #garlic #oliveoil #butter #preserved #peppers #tomatojuice #roastedredpeppers #boil #chickenstock #stock \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Roasted peppers, garlic and couscous in a delicious salad\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1244\n|PortionCalories = 311\n|DatePublished=25th October 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 3 hours, 10 minutes (incl. chilling time)\n |PrepTime = 3 hours\n |CookTime = 10 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Couscous, red pepper and garlic salad recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Tasted authentic</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.25</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">I think the roasted peppers made all the difference.</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Sue_spins|Susie]] </span></span>\n}}\nThe [[Peppers|peppers]] and [[Garlic|garlic]] are [[Roasted|roasted]].  [[Preserved]] [[Roasted red peppers|roasted red peppers]] such as [[Bell peppers#Pimientos del Piquillo de Lodosa|Pimientos del Piquillo de Lodosa]] are excellent for this recipe and a great time saver.  The recipe has no particular country of origin, but its flavours are a combination of [[Spanish]] and Maghreb\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 2 bulbs [[Garlic|garlic]], separated into [[Cloves|cloves]] and peeled\n| 80 ml [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 2 large [[Roasted sweet peppers|red peppers, roasted]] and peeled or [[Preserved|preserved]], and cut into strips\n| 380 ml [[Vegetable|vegetable]] or [[Chicken stock|chicken stock]]\n| 180 g [[Couscous|couscous]]\n| 90 g melted [[Butter|butter]]\n}}\n'''For the dressing'''\n* 125 ml [[Gazpacho ligero con mostaza]] or [[Tomato juice|tomato juice]]\n* 1 tablespoon [[Sherry vinegar|sherry vinegar]]\n* 1&frac12; teaspoons [[Harissa|harissa]]\n* 60 ml [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n* 4 tablespoons [[Herbs|herbs]], finely chopped, eg. [[Chives|chives]], flat-leaved [[Parsley|parsley]]\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to 180\u00b0 C (350\u00b0 F - gas 4) and [[Roast|roast]] the [[Garlic|garlic]] in the [[Oil|oil]] for 25 minutes.\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Bring the [[Stock|stock]] to the [[Boil|boil]] and stir in the cousous.\n| Remove from the heat  and allow to stand until it has absorbed the liquid.\n| Return to heat and stir in the [[Butter|butter]].\n| Allow to cool and add the [[Peppers|peppers]], [[Garlic|garlic]] and dressing.\n| Chill briefly.\n}}\n'''To make the dressing'''\n# Place all the ingredients in a jar and shake until blended\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Couscous, pepper and garlic salad]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments|Couscous, pepper and garlic salad]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes|Couscous, pepper and garlic salad]]\n[[Category:North African recipes|Couscous, pepper and garlic salad]]\n[[Category:Salad recipes|Couscous, pepper and garlic salad]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes|Couscous, pepper and garlic salad]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes|Couscous, pepper and garlic salad]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]][[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#couscouspepperandgarlicsalad #garlic #oliveoil #butter #preserved #peppers #tomatojuice #roastedredpeppers #boil #chickenstock #stock </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

[[Chives|chives]], flat-leaved [[Parsley|parsley]]\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Add the [[oil]] and the peeled [[garlic]] to the bowl '''20 minutes / Temp. Varoma / Speed Spoon / Reverse blade / MC Off'''\n| Remove and strain the [[oil]] reserving it and the [[garlic]]\n| Make the dressing - see below\n| Add the [[Stock|stock]] '''4 minutes / 100\u00b0 C / Speed 1'''\n| Stir in the [[couscous]] '''2 minutes / 100\u00b0 C / Speed 1 / Reverse blade'''\n| Allow to stand until it has absorbed the liquid\n| Stir in the [[Butter|butter]] '''1 minute / 80\u00b0 C / Speed 3 / Reverse blade'''\n| Allow to cool and add the [[Peppers|peppers]], [[Garlic|garlic]] and dressing '''1 minute / Speed 3-4 / Reverse blade'''\n| Chill in the fridge for 2-3 hours\n}}\n'''To make the dressing'''\n# After frying the garlic, chop the herbs '''2-3 seconds / Turbo'''\n# Add all the remaining dressing ingredients, making the reserved oil up to 60g '''10 seconds / Speed 4 / Reverse blade'''\n# Empty the bowl and reserve in the same container as the [[garlic]]\n\n===Chefs notes===\nIf using preserved [[Red peppers|peppers]] do not chop beforehand\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Couscous, pepper and garlic salad]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments|Couscous, pepper and garlic salad]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes|Couscous, pepper and garlic salad]]\n[[Category:North African recipes|Couscous, pepper and garlic salad]]\n[[Category:Salad recipes|Couscous, pepper and garlic salad]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes|Couscous, pepper and garlic salad]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes|Couscous, pepper and garlic salad]]\n[[Category:Thermomix recipes|Couscous, pepper and garlic salad]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes|Couscous, pepper and garlic salad]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]][[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#garlic #couscous #butter #oliveoil #peppers #preserved #spanish #parsley #stock #herbs #redpeppers </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

lunchtime snack.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 675 g (1.5 lb) [[tomatoes]]\n| 1 to 2 [[hard-boiled eggs]] per person\n| 4 [[Garlic|garlic]] cloves, chopped finely\n| 5 tablespoons (75 ml) [[olive oil]]\n| [[dried apricots]], chopped finely\n| 2 [[celery]] sticks, sliced into moons\n| 1 cup [[couscous]]\n| 350 ml (12 fl oz) [[vegetable]] [[stock]] (a veggie stock cube in [[boiled]] water would do ok)\n| Gas 6)\n\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Slice the [[tomatoes]] in two and lay on a [[baking]] tray\n| Drizzle with 2 tablespoons (30 ml) of the [[olive oil]], sprinkle with chopped [[chilli]], [[sugar]], [[salt]] and [[pepper]] - roast for 20 minutes\n| Drop the [[eggs]] into [[boiling]] water, return top the [[boil]] and boil for 4 minutes - remove and plunge into cold water until cold then peel\n| Heat the 2 tablespoons (30 ml) of the [[oil]] in a large pan on a low heat and soften the [[onion]] and [[celery]] until soft, about 5 minutes\n| Add the [[sultana]] and [[couscous]] and [[stir-fry]] for a few minutes\n| Tip in the [[stock]] and [[couscous]] into the pan, cooks for a few minutes then leave, covered so all of the liquid is absorbed into the couscous\n| Add the [[tomatoes]], spices, if using, and remaining 1 tablespoon (15 ml) of [[olive oil]], season to taste and in a [[food processor]], blend to a paste, add a little hot water if it is too dry\n| Arrange the [[eggs]] in a large serving bowl or four separate bowls, spoon half of the [[tomato sauce]] over the [[eggs]], and cover with [[couscous]], sprinkle with [[almond flakes]]\n| Serve with the remaining [[sauce]] in a bowl or gravy boat\n}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Main title": "El ham lahou (Ramadan lamb)",

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=El ham lahou (Ramadan lamb), a fruit recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#lamb #butter #orangeflowerwater #ghee #raisins #almonds #prunes #pear #stock #dried #simmer \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This lamb stew is eaten in Algeria after a day of fasting during Ramadan\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 4003\n|PortionCalories = 1000\n|DatePublished=19th January 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 2 hours 30 minutes\n |PrepTime = 1 hour, 15 minutes\n |CookTime = 1 hour 15 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:El ham lahou (Ramadan lamb) recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Nice</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Love the pear too</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Image:El ham lahou (Ramadan lamb) cooling.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Cooling down]]\nThis [[Lamb|lamb]] [[Stew|stew]] is eaten in Algeria after a day of fasting during Ramadan.  This recipe is served at room temperature, so don't forget to adjust your cooking times accordingly.\n\nHaving mode this delicious dish, it's evident that the [[butter]] or [[ghee]] is an important ingredient in this fairly rich dish,  It would not be the same with less.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 50 g [[Butter|butter]]\n| 900 g [[Lamb|lamb]], cut into 6cm (2&frac12;\u201d) pieces\n| &frac12; teaspoon [[Ground cinnamon|ground cinnamon]]\n| 750 ml water or [[Stock|stock]]\n| 50 g [[Sugar|sugar]]\n| 12 [[Dried|dried]] [[Prunes|prunes]], soaked in water for one hour\n| 2 tablespoons [[Raisins|raisins]]\n| 2 tablespoons whole [[Almonds|almonds]], [[Blanched|blanched]]\n| 1 firm [[Pear|pear]], peeled and cut into [[Wedges|wedges]]\n| 30 ml [[Orange flower water|orange flower water]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Melt the [[Butter|butter]] in a pan, add the [[Lamb|lamb]] and [[Saute|saute]] over low heat for 5 minutes.\n| Add the [[Cinnamon|cinnamon]], water or [[Stock|stock]] and [[Sugar|sugar]] and mix well.\n| Increase the heat to moderate and cook (covered) for about 40 minutes, or until the [[Meat|meat]] is tender.\n| Drain the [[Prunes|prunes]] and add them to the [[Lamb|lamb]] with the [[Raisins|raisins]], [[Almonds|almonds]] and [[Pear|pear]].\n| [[Simmer]] for a further 15 minutes.\n| Remove the pan from the heat and stir in the [[Orange flower water|orange flower water]].\n| Allow to cool a little.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe at room temperature with [[couscous]] or [[Rice|rice]] or [[Salad|salad]] and [[Bread|bread]].\n===Chef's note===\nAs usual, I didn't read the recipe properly when shopping and bought a small [[leg of lamb]].  I removed the meat from the bone, but have included the bone in the cooking process just for the flavour.\n\nI used  a few substitutions when I made this:\n* [[Ghee]] instead of [[butter]]\n* [[jaggery]] instead of sugar\n* The chopped flesh of half an [[orange]] with the grated [[zest]] of a third of an orange instead of the [[Orange flower water|orange flower water]]. \n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|El ham lahou (ramadan lamb)]]\n[[Category:Algerian recipes|El ham lahou (ramadan lamb)]]\n[[Category:Lamb recipes|El ham lahou (ramadan lamb)]]\n[[Category:Main courses|El ham lahou (ramadan lamb)]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes|El ham lahou (ramadan lamb)]]\n[[Category:North African recipes|El ham lahou (ramadan lamb)]]\n[[Category:Stews and casseroles|El ham lahou (ramadan lamb)]]\n[[Category:Fruit recipes]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Stewed, braised or pot roasted]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#lamb #butter #orangeflowerwater #ghee #raisins #almonds #prunes #pear #stock #dried #simmer </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Falafel, Garlic recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#falafel #coriander #pittabread #burghul #chickpeas #lemon #cumin #garlic #zest #jellybag #frying \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Falafel is a fried ball or patty made from spiced fava beans and/or chickpeas\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}}\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1332\n|PortionCalories = 333\n|DatePublished=31st January 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 4\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime = 3 hours\n|PrepTime = 2 hours 45 minutes\n|CookTime = 15 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Falafel.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"><span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">A wonderful mezze</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">3.8</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Great in a pitta with tzatziki</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\">[[User:Chef|Jerry]] </span></span>\n}}\n'''Falafel''' is a fried ball or patty made from spiced [[fava beans]] and/or [[chickpeas]]. It is a popular form of fast food in the Arab World, where it is also served as a mezze.\n\nFalafel is usually served in [[pitta bread]], either inside the pita, which acts as a pocket, or wrapped in a flat pita. In many countries falafel is a popular street food or fast food. The falafel balls, whole or crushed, may be topped with salads, pickled vegetables and hot sauce, and drizzled with [[tahini]]-based sauces. Falafel balls may also be eaten alone as a snack or served as part of a mezze. During Ramadan, they are sometimes eaten as part of an iftar, the meal which breaks the daily fast after sunset.\n\nFalafel has been part of the diet of Egyptians and the people of the Arab World (Muslims, Christians and Mizrahi Jews among them) for centuries.\n\n==Falafel recipe==\n\nYou can buy packets of [[Falafel|falafel]] mixture but it's just as easy to make it yourself, and like all self-made meals, you can adjust the flavours to suit your tastes.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 225 g (8oz) [[Dried|dried]] [[Chickpeas|chickpeas]], soaked overnight in cold water, boiled until soft (about 2 hours) and drained\n| 75 g pitta bread, torn into pieces\n| 75 g fine [[burghul]]\n| 1 small [[onion]], peeled and chopped\n| 1 teaspoon [[Cumin|cumin]] seeds, ground\n| 1 teaspoon [[Coriander|coriander]] seeds, ground\n| 1 - 2 teaspoons [[chilli flakes]] or [[chilli powder]] (or to taste)\n| 1 - 2 [[Garlic|garlic]] cloves, peeled and crushed (or to taste)\n| 1 tablespoon fresh [[coriander]] or [[Parsley|parsley]] leaves and stalks, chopped\n| The juice and [[Zest|zest]] from &frac12; a [[Lemon|lemon]]\n| [[Sea salt]] and freshly ground [[black pepper]] to taste\n| [[Vegetable oil]] for [[Frying|frying]]\n}}\n\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Soak the pitta breads until soft\n| Soak the [[burghul]] for 15 minutes\n| Squeeze as much water out of the [[burghul]] and the [[pitta bread]], you can use a [[jelly bag]] for this\n| In a [[Coffee|coffee]] grinder or [[Mortar and pestle|mortar and pestle]], grind the [[Coriander|coriander]] and [[Cumin|cumin]] seeds.\n| Rinse and drain the [[Chickpeas|chickpeas]] and place in a [[Food processor|food processor]] with the rest of the ingredients \n| Blend until smooth\n| Shape into about 25 balls and refrigerate for 2 hours to allow the flavours to mingle.\n| Heat 5 cm (2\") of [[Oil|oil]] in a frying pan or [[Wok|wok]], or you can use a deep-fat fryer.\n| [[Deep-fry]] in batches for about 4-5 minutes, until [[Browned|browned]]. Remove with a slotted spoon and drain on kitchen paper\n}}\n===Serving suggestion===\n\nServe 3 or 4 falafel inside a warm [[pitta bread]], with a drizzle of [[Yoghurt|yogurt]] or [[garlic mayonnaise]] and a few salad leaves.\n===Variations===\nPersonally, I would add 1-2 bulbs (rather than cloves) of [[Garlic|garlic]], but leave out the [[lemon]] [[zest]].\n\nUse 1 large 400 g can of chickpeas, drained instead of dried chickpeas.\n===Chef's tip===\n\nFalafel freeze well.\n\n==See also==\n* '''[[Falafel with cucumber salad and pitta bread]]'''\n{{RecipeLine}}\n{{CategoryLineIngredients}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes]]\n[[Category:Lebanese recipes]]\n[[Category:Middle Eastern recipes]]\n[[Category:North African recipes]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Ingredients]]\n[[Category:Prepared foods]]\n[[Category:Deep fried]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#falafel #coriander #pittabread #burghul #chickpeas #lemon #cumin #garlic #zest #jellybag #frying </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }
    }
}

could complete them in such a short time!\n\nAnyway, this is my variation on Jamie's [[Falafel]] wraps with [[Grilled|grilled]] veg & [[Salsa|salsa]] - I've made this in 4 person quantity and we'll have this for 2 days.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n}}\n'''falafels'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 400g can of mixed [[Pulses|pulses]] or mixed [[Beans|beans]]\n| 400g can of [[Chickpeas|chickpeas]]\n| [[Zest]] of 1 [[Lemon|lemon]], finely [[Grated|grated]]\n| 1 tablespoon of [[Harissa paste|harissa paste]]\n| 1 teaspoon of [[Cumin seeds|cumin seeds]], freshly [[Ground|ground]]\n| 1 tablespoon of [[Plain flour|plain flour]]\n| 1 tablespoon of [[Olive oil|olive oil]] (for the [[Falafel|falafel]] mix)\n| Pinch of [[Salt|salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]]\n| 1 tablespoon of  [[Olive oil|olive oil]] (to [[Fry|fry]] the falafels)\n| The stems from a bunch of [[Coriander|coriander]], chopped finely and a handful of leaves\n}}\n'''[[Tomato salsa|tomato salsa]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 3 large [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]]\n| 1 fresh [[Chilli|chilli]], finely chopped\n| 1 [[Fat|fat]] [[Clove|clove]] of [[Garlic, peeled and crushed|garlic, peeled and crushed]]\n| [[Juice]] and [[Grated|grated]] [[Zest|zest]] from 1 [[Lime|lime]]\n| [[Salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]] to taste\n}}\n'''[[Grilled|grilled]] [[Vegetables|vegetables]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 1 [[Fennel bulb|fennel bulb]], thinly sliced\n| 1 medium [[Onion|onion]], thinly sliced\n| 2 [[Sweet peppers|sweet peppers]], deseeded and cut into chunks\n| 1 [[Sprig of rosemary|sprig of rosemary]]\n| 1 [[Sprig of mint|sprig of mint]]\n| [[Ground pepper]] to taste \n| [[Salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]] to taste\n}}\n'''[[Side dishes|side dishes]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 1 pack of [[Corn tortillas|corn tortillas]]\n| 300 g tub of [[Cottage cheese|cottage cheese]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Chilli sauce]] of your choice\n| 4 tablespoons of [[Pickled red cabbage|pickled red cabbage]]\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Falafel wraps with grilled veg and salsa and cat.jpg|The spread, cat 'n all!\nImage:Jamies grilled vegetables.jpg|The grilled vegetables after 5 minutes\nImage:Jamies alternate grilled vegetables.jpg|The following day's grilled vegetable variation (''the best'')\n</gallery>\n===Method===\n'''falafels'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Drain the [[Beans|beans]] and [[Chickpeas|chickpeas]] and dry them really well.  A [[Salad spinner|salad spinner]] is a good way to do this.  They need to be really dry or the falafels will not stick together.  \n| Tip them into the [[Food processor|food processor]] with all the [[Falafel|falafel]] ingredients and [[Blend|blend]] to a fairly fine paste\n| Using wetted hands, form the [[Falafel|falafel]] mix into about 12 balls and press them flat so there is a good surface to [[Fry|fry]] and [[Brown|brown]]\n| [[Fry]] then is a tablespoon of [[Olive oil|olive oil]], turn them once they have [[Browned|browned]] , the less you handle them, the less chance these is of them falling apart. Don't worry if they fall apart - mine did!  They are going in a [[Tortilla|tortilla]] wrap anyway.\n}}\n'''[[Grilled|grilled]] [[Vegetables|vegetables]]'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Add a spay of [[Olive oil|olive oil]] to your [[Griddle pan|griddle pan]] and throw in all of the [[Vegetables|vegetables]] for [[Grilling|grilling]] together with the [[Herbs|herbs]]\n| Gill for 10 minutes or more, turning now and then\n| Add the [[Juice|juice]] of half a [[Lemon|lemon]] just before you serve\n}}\n'''[[Salsa|salsa]]'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Add the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], chopped [[Chilli|chilli]], [[Coriander|coriander]] stems and leaves, [[Crushed garlic|crushed garlic]], [[Lime juice|lime juice]] and [[Zest|zest]] and seasoning to the [[Food processor|food processor]] and blitz until it  gets to your desired consistency - chill if you have the time\n}}\n'''[[Cottage cheese|cottage cheese]]'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Stir in a tablespoon of [[Chilli sauce|chilli sauce]] to add some colour and bite\n}}\n'''[[Corn tortillas|corn tortillas]]'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| [[Microwave]] for 45 seconds just to moisten them and warm them a little\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nSpread everything out and tuck in!\n===Recipe source===\n\n* Idea from Jamie Oliver's 15 minute meals TV series\n===Variations===\nTry you own variation on [[Herbs|herbs]] and [[Spices|spices]]\n\n[[Courgettes]] and [[Carrots|carrots]] make a nice change for the [[Grilled|grilled]] vegetables.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Lebanese recipes]]\n[[Category:Middle Eastern recipes]]\n[[Category:North African recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Grilled, griddled or barbecued]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#falafel #grilled #oliveoil #fry #vegetables #zest #herbs #beans #chillisauce #cottagecheese #salsa </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Fatayer",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Fatayer a cheese recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#fatayer #dough #flour #hand #oliveoil #garlic #cheese #breadmaker #squash #wintersquash #yeast \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Fatayer is a pastry that can be stuffed with spinach (sabaneq), cheese (jibnah) or meat\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1165\n|PortionCalories = 291\n|DatePublished=22nd October 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 3\n |TotalTime = 2 hours 30 minutes\n |PrepTime = 2 hours\n |CookTime = 30 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Fatayer recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"><span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Lebanese 'Cornish' pasties</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.2</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Although they could not be sold as such! \ud83d\ude01</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\">[[User:Chef|Jerry]] </span></span>\n}}\nFatayer is a pastry that can be stuffed with [[Spinach|spinach]] (sabaneq), [[Cheese|cheese]] (jibnah) or [[Meat|meat]]. It is part of [[Middle Eastern cuisine]] and is eaten in [[Turkey]], Syria, Lebanon, Jordan and other countries in the region.\n\nThis version using [[Winter squash|winter squash]] is based on a recipe in Sam & Sam Clarkes' excellent '[[Moro]]' cookbook - ISBN 9780091880842\n\n\n'''For the  Fatayer [[Dough|dough]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 220 g [[Strong white bread flour|strong white bread flour]]\n| &#189; teaspoon [[Dried active yeast|dried active yeast]]\n| &#189; teaspoon [[Sugar|sugar]]\n| &#189; teaspoon fine [[Sea Salt|sea salt]]\n| 100 ml (100g) tepid water\n| 2 tablespoons [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n}}\n'''For the Fatayer filling'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 800g [[Orange|orange]] fleshed sweet [[Winter squash|winter squash]] such as Hubbard, Festival, Butternut. Peeled and de-seeded and cut into 5 cm (2\") chunks\n| 1 tablespoon [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 1 Clove of [[Garlic|garlic]], peeled and crushed\n| 100g [[Feta cheese|feta cheese]], crumbled with 1 tablespoon freshly chopped [[Marjoram|marjoram]] or [[Oregano|oregano]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Toasted|toasted]] pinenuts\n| &#188; teaspoon [[Ground cumin|ground cumin]]\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to 230\u00b0 C (450\u00b0 F - gas 8), [fan oven 210\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour]\n===Method===\n\n\n'''Making the fatayer [[Dough|dough]] with a [[Breadmaker|breadmaker]]'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Add all of the [[Dough|dough]] ingredients to your [[Breadmaker|breadmaker]]\n| Set to ''[[Dough|dough]]'' or ''[[Pizza|pizza]]'' setting\n| Wait for an hour , remove the perfect [[Dough|dough]]. If the dough s to wet add a little more [[Flour|flour]] and repeat the cycle, more water if too dry.\n}}\n'''Making the fatayer [[Dough|dough]] by [[Hand|hand]]'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Sift the [[Flour|flour]] into a bowl\n| Warm the water to body temperature.\n| Take a few tablespoons of the warm water, add the [[Sugar|sugar]] and [[Yeast|yeast]] and leave in a warm place for 15 minutes.\n| Stir the [[Salt|salt]] and [[Oil|oil]] into the remaining water.\n| Add the [[Yeast|yeast]] mixture to the [[Flour|flour]]  and little by little, add the remaining water, massaging the lumps out by [[Hand|hand]].\n| Once you have added all of the water and you have a manageable lump, transfer to a [[Flour|flour]]ed surface and [[Kneading bread|knead]] by [[Hand|hand]] for about 10 minutes or until soft and elastic but not tacky.  Add more [[Flour|flour]] or water to get to the correct consistency.\n| Cover with a damp [[Tea-towel|tea-towel]] and leave in a warm place of about an hour.\n'''Preparing the [[Butternut squash|butternut squash]] filling'''\n| Toss the cubed sqush in a bowl with the [[Garlic|garlic]], [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and a grind of [[Black pepper|black pepper]]\n| [[Roast]] on a [[Baking tray|baking tray]] for about 20 minutes or until you can squish the [[Squash|squash]] with your finger.\n| Allow to cool a little and then [[Mash|mash]] to a pur\u00e9e. Season to taste.\n}}\n'''Making the fatayers'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Divide the [[Dough|dough]] into 4 balls.  Roll each ball into an 18cm (7\") disc.\n| Divide the remaining ingredients into four and place in the centre of each disc, [[Squash|squash]] first, [[Cheese|cheese]] last.\n| [[Brush]] the edges of the discs with a little water so they stick better and then shape to a small pyramid and squeeze the joins together to seal.\n| Trim and discard any excess [[Dough|dough]].\n| [[Bake]] for 15 minutes until lightly coloured, but not crisp.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with a [[Green salad|green salad]] and [[Tahini|tahini]].\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Lebanese recipes]]\n[[Category:Libyan recipes]]\n[[Category:Middle Eastern recipes]]\n[[Category:North African recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]][[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#fatayer #dough #flour #hand #oliveoil #garlic #cheese #breadmaker #squash #wintersquash #yeast </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }

title": "Fattoush",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Fattoush, Vegetarian recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#fattoush #vegetables #sumac #diced #herbs #pittabread #fried #lemonjuice #cabbage #parsley #springonions \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Fattoush, pronounced \"fadash\", is a Levantine salad made from several garden vegetables and toasted or fried pieces of pita bread\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1107\n|PortionCalories = 276\n|DatePublished=24th October 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 4\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime = 15 minutes\n|PrepTime = 15 minutes\n|CookTime = None\n|Image = [[Image:Fattoush recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"><span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Delicious veggie meal</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.6</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Thanks Julia - this was superb!</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\">[[User:Chef|Jerry]] </span></span>\n}}\nFattoush, pronounced \"fadash\", is a Levantine [[salad]] made from several garden [[vegetables]] and [[toasted]] or [[fried]] pieces of [[pita bread]]. Fattoush salad allows cooks to use seasonal produce by mixing different [[vegetables]] and [[herbs]] according to taste, and also to make use of pitas that have gone stale. The vegetables are cut into relatively larges pieces compared to [[Tabbouleh]] which requires ingredients to be finely chopped. [[Sumac]] is usually used to give Fattoush its sour taste.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 [[cucumber]], peeled, deseeded and [[diced]]\n| 6 tablespoons [[extra virgin olive oil]]\n| 3 [[pitta breads]], split in two and cut into 2.5 cm (1\") squares\n| 2 tablespoons torn fresh [[coriander leaves]]\n| 2 tablespoons roughly chopped fresh [[mint]]\n| 2 tablespoons roughly chopped fresh [[parsley]]\n| 1 [[red onion]], cut into 1cm/&frac12;in dice\n| 5 ripe [[Tomatoes, roasted and peeled|tomatoes, peeled, deseeded]] and cut into 1cm/&frac12;in dice\n| 2 [[green bell peppers]], deseeded and cut into thin strips\n| 2 [[cloves of garlic, crushed]]\n| 1 tablespoon of [[sumac]] or the juice of 1 [[lemon]]\n| [[Salt]] and [[freshly ground black pepper]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Heat 2 tablespoons of the [[oil]] in a [[frying]] pan and [[fry]] the [[pitta bread]] until it is golden brown. Drain on kitchen paper to remove any excess oil\n| Alternatively, cook the [[pitta bread]] using our [[crisp bread]] recipe, then cut into squares\n| Add the [[Garlic|garlic]], [[lemon juice]], remaining [[olive oil]] and the [[herbs]] into a bowl and mix well to make the dressing\n| Put the [[diced]] [[vegetables]] in a large bowl and pour the dressing over the [[vegetables]] and toss well\n| Season to taste with [[salt]] and [[pepper]], garnish with the strips of [[fried]] [[bread]]\n}}\n===Variations===\n\nThere are many variations for this recipe, some alternative ingredients might be:\n*[[Lettuce]]\n*[[Spring onions]]\n*[[Feta cheese]]\n*[[Carrots]]\n*[[Red peppers]]\n*[[Green peppers]]\n*[[Cabbage]]\n*[[Black olives]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:North African recipes]]\n[[Category:Middle Eastern recipes]]\n[[Category:Salad recipes]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Uncooked]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#fattoush #vegetables #sumac #diced #herbs #pittabread #fried #lemonjuice #cabbage #parsley #springonions </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }
